Our Operations, Security and Engineering teams operate on a 24/7 coverage model to respond to any changes within the markets.</p></div></li></ul></div></div><div data-testid="hero-banner" class="not-card full-bleed css-rwfvxi"><div class="hero-container"><div class="text-container kdFIjO hYZFkb white" data-testid="hero-text-container"><div class="pBpti fPSBzf iRgpoQ pvuga fzpnVj!" data-testid="header-with-sub"><h2 class="cPOeGc fpwqQU jXrpIW eCAgNE jXrpIW hero-headline">Best-in-class security</h2></div><div class="hero-content css-14mqa94" data-testid="richtext-component"><p>Possessing internally maintained security programs is one thing, but having them measure up to industry standards and validating them by achieving best-in-class certifications is another. The latter is much more difficult and time-consuming, but if you want to be a safe company, it is necessary and worthwhile. Our ISO27001 certification proves we do it.</p></div><div data-testid="cta-button-component" class="cta-button-container css-1dg3nil"></div></div><div class="fPSBzf iRgpoQ kdFIjO hYZFkb bYPznK bYPztT"><img alt="Rectangular certification badge on a dark green surface, featuring &quot;LRQA Certified&quot; and &quot;UKAS Management Systems&quot; with ISO/IEC 27001." data-testid="image" loading="lazy" width="1200" height="1200" decoding="async" data-nimg="1" srcset="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fsbcdn.bitpanda.com%2F1200x1200%2Fdfa73c3e7f%2Fbest-in-class-security.png&amp;w=1200&amp;q=75 1x, /_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fsbcdn.bitpanda.com%2F1200x1200%2Fdfa73c3e7f%2Fbest-in-class-security.png&amp;w=3840&amp;q=75 2x" src="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fsbcdn.bitpanda.com%2F1200x1200%2Fdfa73c3e7f%2Fbest-in-class-security.png&amp;w=3840&amp;q=75" style="color: transparent;"><div></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="hero-banner" class="not-card full-bleed css-abhlhm"><div class="hero-container"><div class="text-container kdFIjO hYZFkb white" data-testid="hero-text-container"><div class="pBpti fPSBzf iRgpoQ pvuga fzpnVj!" data-testid="header-with-sub"><h2 class="cPOeGc fpwqQU jXrpIW eCAgNE jXrpIW hero-headline">Secure</h2></div><div class="hero-content css-14mqa94" data-testid="richtext-component"><p>We have attained the SOC 2 Type 1 report.
